        (bn): BatchNorm2d(128, eps=0.001, momentum=0.03, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
        (act): SiLU(inplace=True)
      )
      (1): BaseConv(
        (conv): Conv2d(256, 128, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False)
        (bn): BatchNorm2d(128, eps=0.001, momentum=0.03, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
        (act): SiLU(inplace=True)
      )

        (act): SiLU(inplace=True)
      )
    )
    (l1_loss): L1Loss()
    (bcewithlog_loss): BCEWithLogitsLoss()

  )
